# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
a sum of sequences ^bHBu9Doc

the sum of the terms in a sequence, it is in a way
the sum of partial sequences making up the original
sequence ^Hu9WDqhF

a cartesian plane to represent complex numbers where the x represent the 
real part and the y the immaginary part ^l14vBg0t

regular form with coordinates in the complex plane ^NJkYspAj

the nth rot is the root of a number say z^n = a where
a is a complex number and the roots of unity are such 
roots where a is 1 like z^4=1 ^gZzsGLsK

in the complex plain the roots of a number are equally spaced out ^GKpB14Ht

write in polar form
set the number equal to (r(cos + i sin))ˆn
apply deMoivre's formula
compare the moduly rˆn=
set left part nt=a+2mpi
state in t
find multiple of m from 0 to n-1
combine toghether ^XTVE6Za8
